<Review>I work in the mall and have eaten as this location several times. It's the perfect spot for a burger if you want higher quality than McDonald's but cheaper than Buckhorn. I've worked in food service and know how difficult it is to iron out the initial kinks and get things off the ground. With this location being brand new to the area, they are often slammed with in person and mobile orders, as well as delivery courier orders. But every time I'm there while it's overwhelmingly busy I see how hard the employees are working to do the best the can, the fastest they can.

My overall review lost a star simply because special orders often get overlooked. I usually add vegetables to my Smoke Shack burger and I love getting the chocolate/vanilla shake- but almost every time I'm given just a chocolate shake and often the vegetables are left off. Not a huge deal as there is no up charge for adding on extras. But it would still be nice to get what I order. If I'm observing correctly it looks like some of the shakes are pre made, presumably to save time- but full transparency goes a long way with customers. If there's no time to give me the chocolate/vanilla option, just let me know!

Overall, besides the obvious hiccups that come with a brand new store, I  am happy to continue eating here!  Hoping they continue to grow and fall into a consistent rhythm. I have high hopes! They seem to hire hard workers, and a location is only as good as it's employees.< /Review><pics>None</pics><Resp>{'time': 1605442508156, 'text': 'Thanks for taking the time to leave a review. <gmapID>0x80d94fba02ddc2cb:0x89e5a6c3a3e0b600<//gmapID>< Review>
Update 2/21:  To get the deal, click on the special tab on Papa Johns website.  You get a large two toppings for $9.99.  If you use TMobile Tuesday App for 25% off with code TMT25, you can get it for $7.49.  I guess you really got to read the fine print and navigate around.

-----------------

Papa Johns and T-Mobile team up to mislead consumers on their deals.  The T-Mobile Tuesday app mislead me into thinking I received a free large 1 topping pizza, but it was a gimmick.  Because they have it under "My Stuff" doesn't mean you get to redeem it.

The other deal they have is to get 25% off of your order online for carryout only.  While I was at the store, I check the online price for a large one topping pizza.  It was $18.95.  With 25% off, this leaves a one topping large pizza for about $14.

Well, the deal at the store is 2 large 2 toppings pizza for only $22.  That would price a large two toppings pizza for only $11.  Now, (1) why would anyone go online to order if the price is substantially higher, and (2) what's the purpose of using a coupon from T-Mobile when it is cheaper to go the store and order.

This Papa Johns location is clean and the staffs are friendly, this is not a reflection of them.  However,  I will no longer go to Papa Johns and Uninstall the T-Mobile Tuesday App immediately.  All of the deals on T-Mobile Tuesday have a gimmick, do not use it.<//Review>
